01The Arsenal

Weapons Of Mass Automation

Every module engineered for total server dominance. No compromises.

Security

Anti-Nuke

Military-grade server protection. Auto-detects mass bans, channel wipes, webhook spam, role deletions & instantly neutralizes threats.

Support

Support Ticket System

Fully automated ticket panels with staff routing, transcripts, claim/close controls and DM alerts for your support team.

Intelligence

AI Auto-Responder

Groq-powered conversational AI with smart mentions, internet access & custom triggers. Your server never sleeps.

Entertainment

Music System

High-fidelity playback with queue, loop, seek, shuffle & autoplay. Drop the beat with crystal-clear audio.

Security

Auto-Moderation

Anti-link, anti-spam, anti-caps, anti-invite & mass-mention filters that keep your servers pristine 24/7.

Control

Combat Moderation

Ban, kick, jail, timeout, nuke, purge & lockdown. Full arsenal of moderation firepower at your fingertips.

Engagement

Leveling & Economy

XP-based leveling, boosters, giveaways, invite tracking & birthday celebrations to keep members engaged.

Entertainment

Arcade Games

Chess, Wordle, Connect Four, 2048, Battleship, RPS & more interactive button games built right in.

Commands Vault
